Ó£™","AvailableDevicesNarratorText":"PC,Mobile","TypeTag":"app","RecommendationReason":"","LongDescription":"Famous 'Spite & Malice' card game, also known as Skip-Bo or 'Cat & Mouse'. Win against the computer or friends by place all cards in sequential order from your own pile before your opponent does. Take the top place in the world player rankings.\r\n\r\nGame Features:\r\n- Realistic AI opponents. No cheats!\r\n- Customize your game by choosing the number of opponents, cards in the stockpile and  game difficulty.\r\n- Play online together with friends or family everywhere: Smartphone, PC or Mac.\r\n- Chat with online opponents\r\n- Unlimited undo\r\n- Scoreboard with player rankings\r\n- Resume games after pause\r\n- Help for the beginners\r\n- No frills.\r\n- Browser game at https://skipoid-nexus.appspot.com for PC or Mac.\r\n\r\nGame rules:\r\n\r\nThe object of the game is to be the first player to play out their entire stock pile. \r\nEach player is dealt 10 (20 or 30) cards for their stock pile with only the uppermost card visible, and a hand of five card. \r\nThe shared play area allows up to four build piles, which must be started using either a \"1\" card or a '*', and each player also has up to four personal discard piles. \r\nEach turn the active player draws until he has five cards in hand, and plays on the build piles. He must play either the next card in sequential order or a wild '*' card, using either cards in hand, the top card of his stock pile, or the top card of any of his four discard piles. Although many variations exist for two, three, five or six players, it is most commonly played by four in two partnerships with two standard decks of cards. A turn begins either by drawing the first card from the stock into the player's hand or by picking up the entire discard pile.
